### Economic Tree ###
shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_railroad
	cost = 4

	x = 17
	y = 0

	allow_branch = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = NKRSZC_remove_ind_tree
		}
	}


	available = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_internal_divisions }
			NOT = { has_idea = SZC_internal_divisions }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea }
			NOT = { has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { SZC_war_aftermath_active = yes }
			SZC_war_aftermath_active = no
		}
		605 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		650 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
	}
	offset = {
		x = -1
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Baoding
				has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Officer
			}
		}
	}
	offset = {
		x = -2
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Federalist
		}
	}
	offset = {
		x = -3
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Industrial
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 20 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway"
		605 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			if = {
				limit = { free_building_slots = { building = infrastructure size > 0 } }
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		650 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			if = {
				limit = { free_building_slots = { building = infrastructure size > 0 } }
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		build_railway = {
			level = 1
			start_province = 4925
			target_province = 6999
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway
			bonus = 2
			uses = 1
			category = train_tech
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_New_Commercial_Zones
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_positive_trade_relations_gold
	cost = 3

	relative_position_id = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway
	x = -3
	y = 1

	available = {
		SZC_opium_tier_1_unlocked = yes
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 5 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_New_Commercial_Zones"
		add_ideas = SZC_commercial_expansion_1
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_one_random_civilian_factory = yes
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_The_Yangtze_Lifeline
	icon = GFX_goal_bluewater_navy
	cost = 3

	relative_position_id = SZC_New_Commercial_Zones
	x = -1
	y = 1

	available = {
		SZC_opium_tier_1_unlocked = yes
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_New_Commercial_Zones
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 10 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_The_Yangtze_Lifeline"
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_commercial_expansion_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_commercial_expansion_3
				add_idea = SZC_commercial_expansion_4
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_commercial_expansion_1
				add_idea = SZC_commercial_expansion_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_aat = no }
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
			show_ideas_tooltip = minsheng_shipping
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { mio:CHN_naval_industry_organisation = { is_mio_available = no } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = available_mio_tt
				show_mio_tooltip = CHN_naval_industry_organisation
			}
			mio:CHN_naval_industry_organisation = {
				set_mio_flag = CHN_mio_unlocked
				add_mio_size = 1
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_Study_Production_Innovations
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_production2
	cost = 3

	relative_position_id = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway
	x = -1
	y = 1

	available = {
		SZC_opium_tier_2_unlocked = yes
		650 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_Chengdu_Chongqing_Railway
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 15 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Study_Production_Innovations"
		if = { #has machinery
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_planning_committee_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_planning_committee_2
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_planning_committee_4
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has construction
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_planning_committee_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_planning_committee_3
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_planning_committee_5
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has machinery and construction
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_planning_committee_6 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_planning_committee_6
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_planning_committee_7
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = SZC_industrial_planning_committee_1
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		}
		650 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }

			}
		}
		else_if = { #has increased munitions production

			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6

		}
		else_if = { #has heavy fire tactics and increased munitions production

			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_9
				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_10
			}
		}
		else = {

				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_2
			}
		}

shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_Dedicated_Logistics_Units
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_construction2
	cost = 5

	relative_position_id = SZC_Army_Drills
	x = -3
	y = 2

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_Adopt_Radio_Communications
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Dedicated_Logistics_Units"
		if = { #has operations
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_2
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_5
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has firepower
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_3
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_6
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has production
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_4 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_4
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_7
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has operations and firepower
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_8 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_8
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_11
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has operations and production
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_9 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_9
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_12
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has firepower and production
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_10 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_10
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_13
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has operations, firepower and production
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_14 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_14
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_15
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = SZC_industrial_army_1
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
}

						can_declare_war_on = ROOT
						china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes
						OR = {
							default_attack_AI_trigger = yes
							NOT = {
								is_neighbor_of = ROOT
								any_neighbor_country = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
								any_subject_country = { any_neighbor_country = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
							}
						}
					}
					YUN = {
						can_declare_war_on = ROOT
						china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes
						OR = {
							default_attack_AI_trigger = yes
							NOT = {
								is_neighbor_of = ROOT
								any_neighbor_country = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
								any_subject_country = { any_neighbor_country = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		will_lead_to_war_with = CHI
		will_lead_to_war_with = GXC
		will_lead_to_war_with = HNN
		will_lead_to_war_with = YUN
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Purge_the_Party_State"
			if = {
				limit = {
					can_declare_war_on = CHI
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = CHI decision = china_attack_decision }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					can_declare_war_on = GXC
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = GXC decision = china_attack_decision }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					HNN = { china_is_aligned_with_left_kmt = yes }
					HNN = { is_subject = no }
					NOT = { country_exists = LKT }
					NOT = { country_exists = RKT }
				}
				HNN = { country_event = china_events.7 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_tt
				effect_tooltip = {
					set_temp_variable = { target = HNN }
					china_puppet_TARGET_effect = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					can_declare_war_on = HNN
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = HNN decision = china_attack_decision }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					can_declare_war_on = YUN
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = YUN decision = china_attack_decision }
			}
		}
	}
}

			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_YCP_chinese_stratocracy"
			custom_effect_tooltip = SZC_YCP_chinese_stratocracy_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = SZC_zhang_guotao
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SZC_YCP_chinese_stratocracy_tt2
				SZC_zhang_guotao = {
					promote_character = paternal_autocrat_stratocracy_subtype
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				}
				country_event = {
					id = NKRsichuan.733
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = paternal_autocrat
						popularity = 0.3
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = NKRsichuan.734
				}
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_YCP_legitimacy_5
				add_idea = SZC_YCP_legitimacy_17
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = SZC_YCP_shining_star_of_yellow_syndicalist
		icon = GFX_goal_SZC_YCP_shining_star_of_yellow_syndicalist

		}

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = SZC_YCP_chinese_stratocracy
